***spaniel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spaniel.html>spaniel</a> (88013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">espaigneul</i> (modern French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">épagneul</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">espaignol</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*Hispāniolus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Spanish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Hispānia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Spain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:spaniel.html>spaniel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">spaniels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various small to medium-sized breeds of gun dog having a broad muzzle, long, wavy fur and long ears that hang at the side of the head, bred for flushing and retrieving game.</li>
<li>A cringing, fawning person.
<ul><li><b>1595</b>: Shakespeare, William, <i>The Two <a href = vnd.unilang:gentlemen.html>Gentlemen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:verona.html>Verona</a></i> Act IV, Scene II
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:proteus.html>Proteus</a></i>: Yet, spaniel-like, the more she spurns my love,/The more it grows and fawneth on her still.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spank.html>spank</a> (99589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably imitative.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:spank.html>spank</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">spanks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">spanking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">spanked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To beat, smack or <a href = vnd.unilang:slap.html>slap</a> a person's buttocks, with the bare hand or other object, as punishment, gesture, or form of sexual interaction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To soundly defeat, to trounce.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To hit very hard
<ul><li><b>15 September 2018</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:barney.html>Barney</a> Ronay, <i>The Guardian</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/football/blog/2018/sep/15/finely-tuned-liverpool-are-really-getting-into-jurgen-klopps-groove">Finely tuned Liverpool are really getting into Jürgen Klopp’s groove</a>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:spurs.html>Spurs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a free-kick on the edge of the Liverpool box. Érik Lamela <b>spanked</b> it low into the wall, got the ball back, played it out to Christian Eriksen.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To move rapidly.
<dl><dd><i>The ship <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> really <b>spanking</b> along.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***spatel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spatel.html>spatel</a> (37741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spatula</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> piece</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a diminutive of the Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spatha</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">broad or <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> tool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself coming from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σπάθη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spáthē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a broad wood or metal blade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spatel.html>spatel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">spatels</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">spateltje</b>)

***spaz.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spaz.html>spaz</a> (46421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spastic</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:spaz.html>spaz</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">spazzes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stupid or incompetent person.
<ul><li><b>2006</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tiger_Woods" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tiger Woods">Tiger Woods</a>:
<dl><dd>“I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so in control from tee to green, the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> I’ve played for years… But as soon as I got on the green I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spaz.html>spaz</a></b>.”</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hyperactive person.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tantrum, a fit.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spastic" class="extiw" title="w:Spastic">Spastic</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spastic" class="extiw" title="w:Spastic">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p>The offensiveness of this term and of <i>spastic</i> differs somewhat between the US and the UK. In the UK, they are very offensive. The term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more commonly used in the <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a>.S. but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still offensive to many in the disability community. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spastic</i> for more.<sup id="cite_ref-Lynnequist_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Lynnequist-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">spack</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">spastic</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:spaz.html>spaz</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">spazzes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">spazzing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">spazzed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To have a tantrum or fit.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To malfunction, go on the <a href = vnd.unilang:fritz.html>fritz</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The sense “to malfunction” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only sense that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not insulting to the object, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cognate to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spasm</i> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seize up</i>), but still may cause offense due to connections with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spastic</i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">have a tantrum</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:freak.html>freak</a> out</span></li></ul>
</body>

***spearmint.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spearmint.html>spearmint</a> (72816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>So named from its spiry, not capitate, inflorescence.
</p><p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spear</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mint</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:spearmint.html>spearmint</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">spearmints</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>Mentha spicata</i>, A herb of the mint family, commonly used in herb tea, candy and to treat mild stomach ache.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:specht.html>specht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*speht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spihtaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)peyk-</i>.

***speeksel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:speeksel.html>speeksel</a> (11406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">speecsel</i>, formed from older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spekel</i> by analogy with <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> suffixed with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-sel</i>. The form <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spekel</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spēkila</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spaiklō</i>. From the same root as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuwen.html>spuwen</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Speichel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:speeksel.html>speeksel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>saliva, spit(tle)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:speeltje.html>speeltje</a> (8598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:speel.html>speel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-tje</i> or from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-tje</i> with lengthening of the root vowel.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:speeltje.html>speeltje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:speeltjes.html>speeltjes</a></b>)
</p>

***spektakel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spektakel.html>spektakel</a> (11608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">spectacle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spectaculum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a show, spectacle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spectare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see, behold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">specere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">species</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***spel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a> (826)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spellen.html>spellen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spelletje.html>spelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>game</li>
<li>playing (e.g. of a musical instrument)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The plural form <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:spellen.html>spellen</a></b></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used referring to
</p>
<ul><li>several repetitions of one <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of game (<a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rounds.html>rounds</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:matches.html>matches</a>)</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkele.html>enkele</a> denkspellen <a href = vnd.unilang:gespeeld.html>gespeeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helder.html>helder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadenken.html>nadenken</a>.</i> – After having played a few thinking games he could no longer think clearly.</dd></dl></dd></dl>
<ul><li>the physical accessories needed for particular games</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> gezelschapspellen <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a>.</i> – I have three board games at home.</dd></dl></dd></dl>
<p>The plural form <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a></b></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used referring to
</p>
<ul><li>different <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of games</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:speel.html>Speel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> gezelschapspelen?</i> – Do you like to play board games?</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blinkt.html>blinkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> in denkspelen.</i> – He excels at thinking games.</dd></dl></dd></dl>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a> (401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spēlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spilon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spilōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (a game)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What do you wish to <b>play</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (a musical instrument)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (a role)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:speler.html>speler</a></i>.
